  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {
    background: none;
  }
  a, chops-button, a.button, .button, .linkify {
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: filter 0.3s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.3s ease-in-out;
  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {
    filter: brightness(95%);
  }
  chops-button, a.button, .button {

    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);

  }
  a.button, .button {
    padding: var(--chops-button-padding);
  }
  chops-button i.material-icons, a.button i.material-icons, .button i.material-icons {
    display: block;
    margin-right: 4px;
  }
  chops-button.emphasized, a.button.emphasized, .button.emphasized {
    background: var(--chops-primary-button-bg);
    color: var(--chops-primary-button-color);
    text-shadow: 1px 1px 3px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.25);
  }
  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.
  */
  .medium-heading {
    font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);

          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

          flex-grow: 1;

          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;

          padding: 0;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }

        }

          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);

          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;

          box-sizing: border-box;

        }
        .issue-header-container {

          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;
        }

          min-width: 50%;
          max-width: 1000px;

          min-height: 100%;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);

          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }
        mr-launch-overview {

          }
          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to repro



<span class="line"><!---->Steps to repro<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I used gs://chromium-browser-asan/linux-release/asan-linux-release-982485.zip



<span class="line"><!---->I used gs://chromium-browser-asan/linux-release/asan-linux-release-982485.zip<!----></span>



<br>





101.0.4951.0 (Developer Build) (64-bit) 



<span class="line"><!---->101.0.4951.0 (Developer Build) (64-bit) <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. ./chrome --user-dat-dir=tmp --disable-popup-blocking 



<span class="line"><!---->1. ./chrome --user-dat-dir=tmp --disable-popup-blocking <!----></span>





http://localhost:8000



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://localhost:8000"><!---->http://localhost:8000<!----></a>



<br>





2. add tab to new group 



<span class="line"><!---->2. add tab to new group <!----></span>



<br>





3. select poc2.html



<span class="line"><!---->3. select poc2.html<!----></span>



<br>





4. open More tools->Task Manager and cancel all columns, make task manager no show any info, DON"T CLOSE Task Manager



<span class="line"><!---->4. open More tools-&gt;Task Manager and cancel all columns, make task manager no show any info, DON"T CLOSE Task Manager<!----></span>



<br>





5. click button on poc2.html 



<span class="line"><!---->5. click button on poc2.html <!----></span>



<br>





6. select Task Manager



<span class="line"><!---->6. select Task Manager<!----></span>



<br>

which is mac only.



<span class="line"><!---->which is mac only.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->TableView doesnt seem to prevent the last remaining visible column from becoming invisible...<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->and neither does TaskManagerView...<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->  <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/8292215621c10665a962a4e03accbb5cd2510186



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/8292215621c10665a962a4e03accbb5cd2510186"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/8292215621c10665a962a4e03accbb5cd2510186<!----></a>

commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





8292215621c10665a962a4e03accbb5cd2510186



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/8292215621c10665a962a4e03accbb5cd2510186"><!---->8292215621c10665a962a4e03accbb5cd2510186<!----></a>



<br>





Author: David Pennington <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: David Pennington &lt;<!----></span>





dpenning@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/dpenning@chromium.org"><!---->dpenning@chromium.org<!----></a>





>



<span class="line"><!---->&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





Date: Tue May 10 21:59:08 2022



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Tue May 10 21:59:08 2022<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Prevent TaskManagerView from hiding all columns



<span class="line"><!---->Prevent TaskManagerView from hiding all columns<!----></span>



<br>





... to prevent container overflow.



<span class="line"><!---->... to prevent container overflow.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





TaskManagerView uses a TableView to display it's data. TableView's allow



<span class="line"><!---->TaskManagerView uses a TableView to display it's data. TableView's allow<!----></span>



<br>





columns to be hidden.TableView keeps a vector of those visible columns



<span class="line"><!---->columns to be hidden.TableView keeps a vector of those visible columns<!----></span>



<br>





and indexes into it for rendering the view.



<span class="line"><!---->and indexes into it for rendering the view.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When all of these columns are hidden, then indexes into this vector



<span class="line"><!---->When all of these columns are hidden, then indexes into this vector<!----></span>



<br>





will inherently cause Container Overflows. in order to fix this on mac



<span class="line"><!---->will inherently cause Container Overflows. in order to fix this on mac<!----></span>



<br>





we previously prevented the ability to hide the last visible column, but



<span class="line"><!---->we previously prevented the ability to hide the last visible column, but<!----></span>



<br>





this fix did not carry over to the other views framework platforms.



<span class="line"><!---->this fix did not carry over to the other views framework platforms.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In order to prevent this issue on all platforms and early return is added



<span class="line"><!---->In order to prevent this issue on all platforms and early return is added<!----></span>



<br>





to the TaskManagerView's SetColumnVisibility to prevent this specific



<span class="line"><!---->to the TaskManagerView's SetColumnVisibility to prevent this specific<!----></span>



<br>





case.



<span class="line"><!---->case.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1320307" title="Security: container-overflow in tab group"><!---->Bug: 1320307<!----></a>

Cherrypicking to M102



<span class="line"><!---->Cherrypicking to M102<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





TaskManagerView uses a TableView to display it's data. TableView's allow



<span class="line"><!---->TaskManagerView uses a TableView to display it's data. TableView's allow<!----></span>



<br>





columns to be hidden.TableView keeps a vector of those visible columns



<span class="line"><!---->columns to be hidden.TableView keeps a vector of those visible columns<!----></span>



<br>





and indexes into it for rendering the view.



<span class="line"><!---->and indexes into it for rendering the view.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When all of these columns are hidden, then indexes into this vector



<span class="line"><!---->When all of these columns are hidden, then indexes into this vector<!----></span>



<br>





will inherently cause Container Overflows. in order to fix this on mac



<span class="line"><!---->will inherently cause Container Overflows. in order to fix this on mac<!----></span>



<br>





we previously prevented the ability to hide the last visible column, but



<span class="line"><!---->we previously prevented the ability to hide the last visible column, but<!----></span>



<br>





this fix did not carry over to the other views framework platforms.



<span class="line"><!---->this fix did not carry over to the other views framework platforms.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In order to prevent this issue on all platforms and early return is added



<span class="line"><!---->In order to prevent this issue on all platforms and early return is added<!----></span>



<br>





to the TaskManagerView's SetColumnVisibility to prevent this specific



<span class="line"><!---->to the TaskManagerView's SetColumnVisibility to prevent this specific<!----></span>



<br>





case.



<span class="line"><!---->case.<!----></span>

[1]



<span class="line"><!---->Hello, thank you for this report. Because this issue is not remote exploitable and requires an implausible level of user interaction, the VRP Panel has determined this issue is not a reasonably exploitable security issue and is not a security bug; unfortunately making this report ineligible for a VRP reward. [1]<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





If you can demonstrate this issue in a way that has a higher exploitability potential and is not reliant on the high level of unreasonable and unlikely user interaction, we would greatly welcome that information and happily reassess for a potential VRP reward. 



<span class="line"><!---->If you can demonstrate this issue in a way that has a higher exploitability potential and is not reliant on the high level of unreasonable and unlikely user interaction, we would greatly welcome that information and happily reassess for a potential VRP reward. <!----></span>

comment #30



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c30"><!---->comment #30<!----></a>





 (



<span class="line"><!----> (<!----></span>





issue 1283805



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1283805" title="Heap-buffer-overflow in TableView::OnItemsRemoved"><!---->issue 1283805<!----></a>





) was submitted in January. In mid February (18 February) to be precise, we updated our security and VRP policies (and communicated out to our researcher community on 18 February) that bugs that require a level user interaction that is deemed to be implausible may not be considered security bugs and may not be eligible for VRP rewards. These issues would be moved to Bug status and processed accordingly, including they are not eligible for a CVE as the potential for exploitability is nearly impossible.

These issues would be moved to Bug status and processed accordingly, including they are not eligible for a CVE as the potential for exploitability is nearly impossible.<!----></span>
